Master Level 5
Description Summons Irena to inflicts significant damage to multiple monsters with a single powerful blow. Skill level can be increased depending on your level.

Master Level 10

The damage of Ultimate Explorer minion skills is calculated differently from that of the character.

Show/hide all levels
Passive Adventurer's Curiosity
Master Level 6
Description Your curiosity and attention to detail grants you bonuses to Critical Rate and the chance of adding monsters to your Monster Collection.
This bonus is multiplicative rather than additive.
This Link Skill can be stacked up to 3 times, once for each unique Explorer Bowman job character you have on this world.
Level 1 Chance to add monsters to Monster Collection: +10%, Critical Rate: +3%
6 Chance to add monsters to Monster Collection: +35%, Critical Rate: +10%

Active Double Jump
Master Level 10
Description Allows you to use the Double Jump skill to move very quickly. Double-tap the up arrow key to jump again while in mid-air. Double-tap the down arrow key to descend more quickly. If you use Action Customization, you can move up in the air with the up arrow and jump keys, and descend with the down arrow and jump keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF.
Level 1 MP Cost: 28, allows you to jump a greater distance
10 MP Cost: 10, allows you to jump a greater distance

Active Covering Fire
Master Level 9
Description Fire arrows while leaping backwards. While firing, you'll have 100% Knockback Resistance. If you press and hold the skill key, you will fire arrows rapidly while in mid-air. You will temporarily not be pushed back by any attack after casting.
Level 1 MP Cost: 3, if you press and hold the skill key after jumping a certain distance backward, you will attack enemies at up to 81% of damage for 2 sec while in mid-air
9 MP Cost: 5, if you press and hold the skill key after jumping a certain distance backward, you will attack enemies at up to 105% of damage for 2 sec while in mid-air

Passive Final Attack : Bow
Master Level 20
Description Chance to deliver an additional hit after a direct attack. Must have a bow equipped.
Required Skill: Bow Mastery Lv. 3
Level 20 required to learn Advanced Final Attack
Level 1 [Final Attack Skill] Has a 2% chance to deal a final attack that deals 100% damage.
20 [Final Attack Skill] Has a 40% chance to deal a final attack that deals 150% damage.

Path of the Ranger

Show/hide all levels
Active Arrow Blaster
Master Level 20
Description Shoot an arrow at a high angle. If you press and hold the skill key, you will fire continuously. While firing, press Up or Down to control the force of the shot.
While casting the skill, press the Interact/Harvest key to set up an Arrow Blaster--which fires arrows automatically--at your location. With Action Customization enabled, you can set up the Arrow Blaster by pressing the attack key, instead of the Interact/Harvest key.
Unaffected by attack reflection.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF.
Level 1 MP Cost: 5, Max Enemies Hit: 4, Damage: 124%. While casting, use the Interact/Harvest key to set up Arrow Blaster, firing arrows that deal 66% damage for 22 sec.
Cooldown for installed Arrow Blaster: 5 sec.
20 MP Cost: 7, Max Enemies Hit: 4, Damage: 181%. While casting, use the Interact/Harvest key to set up Arrow Blaster, firing arrows that deal 85% damage for 60 sec.
Cooldown for installed Arrow Blaster: 5 sec.

Show/hide all levels
Active Speed Mirage
Master Level 20
Description Fire arrows fast enough to leave afterimages.
After striking enemies with enough arrow-based attacks, creates afterimages that fires enemy-seeking arrows before vanishing. These arrows target a single enemy in front of the afterimage and damage any foes pierced on the way to the target. Arrow Blaster turret placement attacks don't count toward this skill's prerequisites.
Empowers Wind Arrow.
Can be toggled On/Off.
Level 1 MP Cost: 90. After successfully striking enemies 12 times with arrow-based attacks, creates 3 afterimages that fire an arrow towards an enemy ahead of them.

Every 7 hits with Arrow Blaster, Hurricane, Silhouette Mirage, Inhuman Speed, Quiver Barrage, and Storm of Arrows count as 1 successful arrow-based strike.
Fired arrows pierce up to 5 enemies and deal 325% damage 4 times on the way to its intended target.

Cooldown: 1 sec

[Passive Effect] Increases Wind Arrow's Range and Damage by 51%p.
20 MP Cost: 90. After successfully striking enemies 12 times with arrow-based attacks, creates 3 afterimages that fire an arrow towards an enemy ahead of them.

Active Speed Mirage
Master Level 20
Description Fire arrows fast enough to leave afterimages.
After striking enemies with enough arrow-based attacks, creates afterimages that fires enemy-seeking arrows before vanishing. Arrow Blaster turret placement attacks don't count toward this skill's prerequisites.

Active Erda Nova
Master Level 25
Description Collect Erda from within yourself and from the surrounding area, then detonate it around your enemies. The Erda of attacked enemies will become disrupted, which will bind their movements. Can deal damage to enemies even when they are under Attack Ignore. Also ignores Attack Reflection.
Level 1 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP, Damage: 156%, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Number of Attacks: 5, Bind Duration: 10 sec.
Bind Duration increases by up to 100% based on damage inflicted with Erda Nova.
Cooldown: 216 sec.

Active Erda Shower
Master Level 25
Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.
Pressing the skill key with the down arrow key summons an Erda Fountain, an object filled with pure Erda.
With Action Customization enabled, you can summon Erda Fountain by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF
Level 1 HP Cost: 3000
Erdas Shower
Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 6, Cooldown reduced by 2 sec per attacked enemy

Erda Fountain

Cooldown: 60 sec
Cooldown shared with Erdas Shower and Erda Fountain.

Active Decent Holy Fountain
Master Level 25
Description Summon a Holy Fountain that restores party members' HP. Even party members with the Undead status can use it. Approach the fountain and press the up arrow key to heal.
Can't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain or Decent Holy Fountain already exists.
If the Decent Holy Fountain disappears before its duration ends, a Vestige of Divinity will remain. cCan't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain, Decent Holy Fountain, or Vestige of Divinity already exists.
Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase recovery skill potency, or increase summon duration. Cannot be summoned near a portal.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 31 sec, restores 5% HP when used, able to use 5 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 89 sec

Active Storm of Arrows
Master Level 25
Description Arrows shot into the sky fall like rain. Unaffected by attack reflection. Has no effect in towns.
Level 1 MP Cost: 1000, Damage: +15%, Duration: 41 sec. Arrows rain down on a zone every 5 sec for 2.5 sec when you attack with your own skills. Up to 6 of these zones can be created, but they cannot overlap.
The falling arrows deal 728% damage to up to 10 enemies, 7 times. If currently attacking more than one enemy, the number of attacks increases by 2 for each additional enemy, for up to 8 additional attacks.
Has 2x more of a chance than Quiver Cartridge does to activate Magic Arrow on attacks in this area.
Cooldown: 120 sec.

Active Inhuman Speed
Master Level 25
Description [Active Effect] Causes you to attack so quickly you produce afterimages. Unaffected by attack reflection. [Passive Effect] After performing a certain number of attacks while the active effect of the skill isn't active, an afterimage is created that attacks for a short time.
Level 1 MP Cost: 800, Max Duration: 30 sec. Fire arrows at set intervals, dealing 416% 3 times to enemies within range of your afterimages, for 3 sec., during the buff.
When the attack hits, Afterimage Attack Duration: +3 sec every 1 sec.
When the attack duration ends, afterimages stop attacking.
Cooldown: 120 sec.

Active Quiver Barrage
Master Level 25
Description Fire every type of arrowhead at once, including a special flaming arrowhead that explodes when it hits an enemy. The Flaming Arrow targets the boss with the highest HP first and is unaffected by attack reflection. The Flaming Arrow is prepared in limited quantities and will no longer attack once used up.
Level 1 MP Cost: 1000. Duration: 40 sec. Final Damage: +15%. Attack Power: + 5%. Fire every type of arrowhead at once, including a flaming arrowhead.
Flaming Arrow: Launches 6 flaming arrows consecutively. Duration: 5 sec., Enemies Hit: 6, Damage: 260%, Number of Attacks: 9, fires 6 flaming arrows up to 18 times. The attack won't activate if the buff remains when all the prepared flaming arrows are consumed. Cooldown: 2 sec.
Cooldown: 120 sec.
25 MP Cost: 1000. Duration: 40 sec. Final Damage: +15%. Attack Power: + 17%. Fire every type of arrowhead at once, including a flaming arrowhead.

Active Silhouette Mirage
Master Level 25
Description Evades enemy attacks by moving fast enough to create illusory doubles of yourself.
Illusory doubles disperse the enemy's attention to either reduce damage taken by Bow Master or inflict damage on the enemy. The time to create the illusory doubles isn't deducted when you are incapacitated. Illusory doubles are unaffected by attack reflection.
Can be toggled On/Off.
Level 1 Creates up to 2 illusory doubles every 50 sec.
When you either receive damage that is at least 50% of your Max HP or you receive damage that leads to death, 1 illusory double disappears, reducing that damage by 32%
If you have even 1 illusory double, and there is an enemy to attack nearby, when using an attack skill, 5 illusory bullets will deal 416% damage 3 times. MP Cost: 80, Cooldown: 7.5 sec
Cooldown: 1.5 sec
25 Creates up to 2 illusory doubles every 50 sec.
When you either receive damage that is at least 50% of your Max HP or you receive damage that leads to death, 1 illusory double disappears, reducing that damage by 80%
If you have even 1 illusory double, and there is an enemy to attack nearby, when using an attack skill, 5 illusory bullets will deal 800% damage 3 times. MP Cost: 80, Cooldown: 7.5 sec
Cooldown: 1.5 sec

When you either receive damage that is at least 50% of your Max HP or you receive damage that leads to death, 1 illusory double disappears, reducing that damage by 90%
If you have even 1 illusory double, and there is an enemy to attack nearby, when using an attack skill, 5 illusory bullets will deal 880% damage 3 times. MP Cost: 80, Cooldown: 7.5 sec
Cooldown: 1.5 sec

Active Sol Janus: Dusk
Master Level 30
Description Automatically release the Sol Erda within. The energy drawn to the Sol Erda solidifies into Primal Crystals that fall from above.
Primal Crystals are unaffacted by attack reflection. Dusk's cooldown cannot be reduced.

Lv. 30: Normal Enemy Damage: +30%
Level 1 HP Cost: 1% of Max HP
Attacking enemies releases Sol Erda that creates 9 Primal Crystals.
Primal Crystal - Damage: 600%, Number of Attacks: 6
Cooldown: 3 sec
15 HP Cost: 1% of Max HP
Attacking enemies releases Sol Erda that creates 10 Primal Crystals.
Primal Crystal - Damage: 810%, Number of Attacks: 6
Cooldown: 3 sec
30 HP Cost: 1% of Max HP
Attacking enemies releases Sol Erda that creates 11 Primal Crystals.
Primal Crystal - Damage: 1035%, Number of Attacks: 6
Cooldown: 3 sec

Active Sol Janus: Dawn
Master Level 30
Description Summon a Cyclic Ring that endlessly creates and destroys Sol Erda. The cycling Erda Flow attacks nearby enemies.
When a new ring is summoned, the Erda Flow of each ring is reduced. Cyclic rings can be summoned in midair but can't be summoned too close to or too far from an existing ring.
Cyclic Rings are unaffected by attack reflection.

Lv. 30: Normal Monster Damage: +30%
Level 1 HP Cost: 10% of Max HP
Ring Duration: 60 sec, Max Number of Rings: 1
Cyclic Ring - Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 400%, Number of Attacks: 6
Cooldown: 60 sec
9 HP Cost: 10% of Max HP
Ring Duration: 60 sec, Max Number of Rings: 1
Cyclic Ring - Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 480%, Number of Attacks: 6
Cooldown: 60 sec

Ring Duration: 70 sec, Max Number of Rings: 2
Cyclic Ring - Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 490%, Number of Attacks: 6
Cooldown: 60 sec

Ring Duration: 70 sec, Max Number of Rings: 2
Cyclic Ring - Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 580%, Number of Attacks: 6
Cooldown: 60 sec

Ring Duration: 80 sec, Max Number of Rings: 3

Active Ascendant Shadow
Master Level 30
Description Unleashes a barrage of arrows that eclipses the sun. Strikes the enemy periodically with a flurry of arrows. Unaffected by attack reflection.

Lv. 10 - Ignore Defense: +20%
Lv. 20 - Boss Damage: +20%
Lv. 30 - Ignore Defense: +30%, Boss Damage: +30%
Level 1 MP Cost: 1000, Invincible during casting
Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 729%, Number of Attacks: 14, Arrow Flurries: 39

Cooldown: 360 sec
30 MP Cost: 1000, Invincible during casting
Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 1425%, Number of Attacks: 14, Arrow Flurries: 39

Cooldown: 360 sec

Mastery Skills

Mastery Skills are affected by Hyper Skill passives (if applicable) and Boost Node enhancements applied to the base skill.

Show/hide all levels
Active HEXA Hurricane
Master Level 30
Description Launches a catastrophic swarm of arrows at tremendous speed. Targets the enemy with the highest Max HP.
Obtain a special arrowhead from the enemy every time the arrows hit. Once a certain number of special arrowheads are gathered, press Interact/Harvest during the skill to enter shootout mode, which fires even more arrows at once. Enter shootout mode automatically when you gather the max number of special arrowheads.
Shootout Mode can be canceled by pressing Interact/Harvest.
With Action Customization enabled, you can change modes by pressing the attack key, instead of Interact/Harvest.
Can move and use Quiver Cartridge while using this skill.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF
Required Skill: Hurricane Lv. 30
Level 1 MP Cost: 12, Damage: 372% per shot
Obtain 1 special arrowhead when attack hits, Max Special Arrowheads Obtained: 75
When you obtain 40 special arrowheads, you can switch to Shootout Mode
Shootout Mode - MP Cost: 12, consumes 1 special arrowhead when attack hits to fire even more arrows at once, Damage: 489% per shot
30 MP Cost: 12, Damage: 575% per shot
Obtain 1 special arrowhead when attack hits, Max Special Arrowheads Obtained: 75
When you obtain 40 special arrowheads, you can switch to Shootout Mode
Shootout Mode - MP Cost: 12, consumes 1 special arrowhead when attack hits to fire even more arrows at once, Damage: 750% per shot

Active HEXA Arrow Blaster
Master Level 30
Description Shoot an arrow at a high angle. If you press and hold the skill key, you will fire continuously. While firing, press Up or Down to control the force of the shot.
While casting the skill, press the Interact/Harvest key to set up an Arrow Blaster--which fires arrows automatically--at your location. With Action Customization enabled, you can set up the Arrow Blaster by pressing the attack key, instead of the Interact/Harvest key.
Unaffected by attack reflection.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization On/Off.
Required Skill: Arrow Blaster Lv. 20
Level 1 MP Cost: 7, Max Enemies Hit: 4, Damage: 240%.
While casting, use the Interact/Harvest key to set up Arrow Blaster, firing arrows that deal 208% damage for 60 sec.
Cooldown for installed Arrow Blaster: 5 sec.
30 MP Cost: 10, Max Enemies Hit: 4, Damage: 530%.
While casting, use the Interact/Harvest key to set up Arrow Blaster, firing arrows that deal 440% damage for 60 sec.
Cooldown for installed Arrow Blaster: 5 sec.

Enhancements

Enhancements require the corresponding V Skill to be leveled to max and equipped. Final Damage bonuses from Enhancements increase linearly each level, with a jump at levels 10, 20, and 30.
